# ::id nw.chtb_0155.4 ::date 2012-12-05T18:30:47 ::annotator UCO-AMR-03 ::preferred

                  :consist-of (c2 / crane
                        :mod (g / gantry)
                        :mod (t4 / type
                              :mod (w / wheel)))))
      :ARG2 (p / project))

# ::id nw.chtb_0155.5 ::date 2012-12-05T18:37:42 ::annotator UCO-AMR-03 ::preferred
# ::snt The Brazilian side will pay a deposit of 15 % in advance , with the remaining 85 % of payments to be repaid in 8 years .
# ::save-date Wed Dec 5, 2012 ::file nw_chtb_0155_5.txt
(a / and
      :op1 (p / pay-01
            :ARG0 (s / side
                  :mod (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "Brazil")))
            :ARG1 (d / deposit-01
                  :ARG1 (p2 / percentage-entity :value 15))
            :time (i / in
                  :op1 (a2 / advance)))
      :op2 (r / repay-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (t / thing
                  :ARG1-of (p3 / pay-01)
                  :ARG1-of (i2 / include-91
                        :ARG2 (t2 / thing
                              :ARG1-of (p5 / pay-01))
                        :ARG3 (p4 / percentage-entity :value 85))
                  :ARG1-of (r2 / remain-01))
            :time (a / after
                  :op1 (n2 / now)
                  :quant (t3 / temporal-quantity :quant 8
                        :unit (y / year)))))

# ::id nw.chtb_0155.9 ::date 2012-12-05T19:17:48 ::annotator UCO-AMR-03 ::preferred
# ::snt For this , in 1998 China 's Central Treasurer allocated 100 million US dollars as risk preparation funds , to be used by the China Protection Group to launch export credit insurance services .
# ::save-date Mon Sep 16, 2013 ::file nw_chtb_0155_9.txt
(a / allocate-01
      :ARG0 (p2 / person
            :ARG0-of (h / have-org-role-91
                  :ARG1 (c4 / country :name (n3 / name :op1 "China"))
                  :ARG2 (c5 / central-treasurer)))
      :ARG1 (m / monetary-quantity :quant 100000000
            :unit (d / dollar
                  :mod (c / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "US")))
            :domain (t2 / thing
                  :ARG2-of (f / fund-01)
                  :ARG1-of (p / prepare-02
                        :ARG2 (r / risk-01))))
      :ARG2 (o / organization :name (n / name :op1 "China" :op2 "Protection" :op3 "Group"))
      :purpose (t / this)
      :purpose (u / use-01
            :ARG0 o
            :ARG2 (l / launch-01
                  :ARG1 (s / serve-01
                        :ARG1 (i / insure-02
                              :mod (c2 / credit-02
                                    :mod (e / export-01))))))
      :time (d2 / date-entity :year 1998))

# ::id nw.chtb_0155.10 ::date 2012-12-06T17:34:50 ::annotator UCO-AMR-03 ::preferred
# ::snt To date , the Property Insurance Co. of PICC has provided national export corporations with more than 5 billion US dollars of export receipt risk insurance , among which are 170,000 projects for short term export business and over 40 projects for medium to long term projects .
# ::save-date Thu Dec 6, 2012 ::file nw_chtb_0155_10.txt
(p / provide-01
      :ARG0 (c2 / company :name (n2 / name :op1 "Property" :op2 "Insurance" :op3 "Co." :op4 "of" :op5 "PICC"))
      :ARG1 (m / monetary-quantity
            :ARG2-of (i / insure-02
                  :ARG1 (t / thing
                        :ARG2-of (i2 / include-91
                              :ARG1 (a / and
                                    :op1 (p2 / project :quant 170000
                                          :purpose (b / business
                                                :mod (e3 / export-01
                                                      :duration (t2 / term
                                                            :mod (s / short)))))
                                    :op2 (p3 / project
                                          :quant (o / over :op1 40)
                                          :purpose (p4 / project
                                                :duration (t3 / term
                                                      :mod (r3 / range-01
                                                            :ARG3 (m3 / medium)
                                                            :ARG4 (l / long))))))))
                  :ARG4 (r / risk-01)
                  :mod (r2 / receipt
                        :mod (e2 / export-01)))
            :quant (m2 / more-than :op1 5000000000)
            :unit (d / dollar
                  :mod (c3 / country :name (n3 / name :op1 "US"))))
      :ARG2 (c / corporation
            :ARG0-of (e / export-01)
            :mod (n / nation)))
